showName, offerCode) {\n                var baseUrl = productUrlStart.replace(\"offerCode\", offerCode);\n                var offerLink = \"\";\n                var query = \"\";\n                if (pageNum !== null && pageNum !== undefined && pageNum <= 0) {\n                    query = 'OnAirNowPg-' + showName + offerCode;\n                    offerLink = baseUrl + '?icid=' + query + '&cm_re=' + query;\n                } else {\n                    query = 'OnAirLastPg' + pageNum + '-' + showName + '-' + offerCode;\n                    offerLink = baseUrl + '?icid=' + query + '&cm_re=' + query;\n                }\n                return offerLink;\n            }\n\n            function updateLinks(links) {\n                //Now increment all the indicies - each item needs to move over by one (and the last one drops off)\n                $.each(links,\n                    function(index, link) {\n                        if (link.href.indexOf(\"OnAirNowPg\") > -1) {\n                            var pattern = /(.*OnAirNowPg)(.*OnAirNowPg)(.*)/;\n                            link.href = link.href.replace(pattern,\n                                function(match, beginning, middle, end) {\n                                    return beginning.replace(\"OnAirNowPg\", \"OnAirLastPg1\") +\n                                        middle.replace(\"OnAirNowPg\", \"OnAirLastPg1\") +\n                                        end;\n                                });\n                        } else {\n                            var pattern = /(.*OnAirLastPg)([0-9]+)(.*OnAirLastPg)([0-9]+)(.*)/;\n                            link.href = link.href.replace(pattern,\n                                function(match, beginning, pageNumber, middle, pageNumber2, end) {\n                                    var pageNum = parseInt(pageNumber) + 1;\n                                    return beginning + pageNum + middle + pageNum + end;\n                                });\n                        }\n                    });\n\n            }\n\n            $(document).on(\"click\",\n                \".on-air-product-buy-now\",\n
